- [Blip](markdown/P_Rage_Blip_Handle.htm.md)

### Finding Methods by Class

Methods are grouped by class. Look for sections like:
- **Methods - Vehicle** — All Vehicle class methods
- **Methods - Ped** — All Ped class methods
- **Methods - Entity** — All Entity class methods

### Namespace Overview

All RPH classes are in the **Rage** namespace. See the Namespaces section for namespace documentation.
